***униматься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:униматься.html>унима́ться</a> (9797)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">унима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">unimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:униматься.html>унима́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">unimátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уняться.html>уня́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow quiet, to quiet down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:униматься.html>унима́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne <b>unimájetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there's no stopping/calming/quietening him</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to abate, to stop</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">унима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">unimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">унима́ть</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">unimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унять.html>уня́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">unjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ять</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***унитаз.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:унитаз.html>унита́з</a> (9367)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">unitas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with the final consonant perhaps influenced by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таз.html>таз</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taz</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pelvis</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <i>Unitas</i> was originally introduced as the name of an early water closet invented by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Twyford" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Thomas Twyford">Thomas Twyford</a> in 1884.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унитаз.html>унита́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">unitáz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унитаз.html>унита́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унитаз.html>унита́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унитаз.html>унита́зов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>toilet (ceramic bowl), flush toilet, water closet</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сортир.html>сорти́р</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sortír</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сральник</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sralʹnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(vulgar)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bélyj drug</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:телефон.html>телефо́н</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bélyj telefón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горшок.html>горшо́к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">goršók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">očkó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толчок.html>толчо́к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tolčók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***уничтожать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уничтожать.html>уничтожа́ть</a> (4898)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уничтожить.html>уничто́жить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uničtóžitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уничтожать.html>уничтожа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uničtožátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уничтожить.html>уничто́жить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to destroy, to annihilate, to obliterate</li>
<li>to abolish, to do away with</li>
<li>to crush</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уничтожать.html>уничтожа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uničtožátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уничтожаться.html>уничтожа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uničtožátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">уничто́житься</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disappear, to go missing</li>
<li>to cease to exist</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уничтожать.html>уничтожа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uničtožátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***уничтожить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уничтожить.html>уничто́жить</a> (2016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ничто́ж(ный)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ničtóž(nyj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уничтожить.html>уничто́жить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uničtóžitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уничтожать.html>уничтожа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to destroy, to annihilate, to obliterate, to wipe out, to blot out, to crush
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>цель</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:уничтоженный.html>уничто́жена</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">A celʹ <b>uničtóžena</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">And the target is <b>annihilated</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to abolish, to do away with</li>
<li>to crush <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">morally</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уносить.html>уноси́ть</a> (5913)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уносить.html>уноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">unosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унести.html>унести́</a></b>)
</p>

***унтер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:унтер.html>у́нтер</a> (15932)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Abbreviation of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у́нтер-офице́р</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">únter-oficér</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унтер.html>у́нтер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">únter</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унтер.html>у́нтера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унтер.html>у́нтеры</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унтер.html>унтера́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унтер.html>у́нтеров</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унтер.html>унтеро́в</a><sup>*</sup></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Dated.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> NCO, noncommissioned officer</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:унывать.html>уныва́ть</a> (16244)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">уны́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">unýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унывать.html>уныва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">unyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">уны́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lose heart, to be cast down, to be dejected or depressed

***уныло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:унылый.html>уны́ло</a> (6946)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унылый.html>уны́лый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">unýlyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унылый.html>уны́ло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">unýlo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>dejectedly, despondently</li>
<li>dismally, cheerlessly</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>gloomy, depressing, bleak

***уныние.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уныние.html>уны́ние</a> (11267)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уныние.html>уны́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">unýnije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уныние.html>уны́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уныние.html>уны́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уныние.html>уны́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gloom, melancholy, dismay
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we date this quote?)</span>,  Alexander Pushkin,  “На <a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>холмах</a> Грузии  | On the Hills of Georgia | ”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://max.mmlc.northwestern.edu/~mdenner/Demo/texts/on_hills_georgia.htm">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><b>уны́нья</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моего́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничто́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чит</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тревожить.html>трево́жит</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Unýnʹja</b> mojevó, ništó ne múčit, ne trevóžit.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">My melancholy, remains untouched and undisturbed.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***унять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:унять.html>уня́ть</a> (12914)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унять.html>уня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">unjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">унима́ть</b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унять.html>уня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">unjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:упадок.html>упа́док</a> (12049)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">упад-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">upad-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упадок.html>упа́док</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">upádok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упадок.html>упа́дка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упадок.html>упа́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упадок.html>упа́дков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>decline, decay, decadence
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приходить.html>приходи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:упадок.html>упа́док</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prixodítʹ v <b>upádok</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to decay</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:состояние.html>состоя́нии</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:упадок.html>упа́дка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v sostojánii <b>upádka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in decline</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:состояние.html>состоя́ния</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:упадок.html>упа́дка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do sostojánija <b>upádka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to a state of decline</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>collapse, breakdown
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упадок.html>упа́док</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>ду́ха</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>upádok</b> dúxa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">despondency; low spirits; depression</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паковать.html>пакова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pakovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упаковать.html>упакова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">upakovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паковать.html>пакова́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упаковывать.html>упако́вывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pack <i>(up)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:упаковать.html>упакова́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вещь.html>ве́щи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чемодан.html>чемода́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>upakovátʹ</b> véšči v čemodán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pack (up) things in/into a suitcase</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упаковать.html>упакова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">upakovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упаковка.html>упако́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">upakóvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упаковка.html>упако́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упаковка.html>упако́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упаковка.html>упако́вок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(action)</i> packing, wrapping</li>
<li><i>(material)</i> wrapping, wrapper, packing, packaging
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вакуумный.html>ва́куумная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:упаковка.html>упако́вка</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vákuumnaja <b>upakóvka</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">vacuum packing</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подарочный.html>пода́рочная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:упаковка.html>упако́вка</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podáročnaja <b>upakóvka</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">gift wrapping</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>цена́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:упаковка.html>упако́вки</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">cená bez <b>upakóvki</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">packing not included</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
